<h2 class="gb-headline gb-headline-56f96671 gb-headline-text header"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="about-us"></span>About Us<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>


<p class="has-base-3-color has-text-color">Founded in 2015, Golfer Geeks was born out of love for the game and the desire to share that passion with others. What began as a single-writer hobby has grown consistently over the years and now garners around 8000 visitors each day. Our growth led us to expand our team to include a PGA pro, a certified club fitter, and soon, another PGA teaching pro and club fitter.<br></p>


<p class="has-base-3-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-0dce5b167da439983f9fda9ba4cd468d">With an experienced team of golf lovers including our founder, a PGA pro, and a certified club fitter, we provide hands-on experience and honest insights that help our readers make the best decisions about their golfing needs. </p>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
// Function to remove active class from all TOC links
    function removeActiveClasses() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.ez-toc-link').forEach(link => {
            link.classList.remove('active');
            const parentLevel3 = link.closest('.ez-toc-list-level-3');
            if (parentLevel3) {
                parentLevel3.classList.remove('has-active-link');
            }
        });
    }

    // Intersection Observer Callback
    const callback = (entries, observer) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                removeActiveClasses();
                // Updated to handle IDs starting with a digit
                const activeLink = document.querySelector(`.ez-toc-link[href="#${entry.target.id}"]`);
                if (activeLink) {
                    activeLink.classList.add('active');
                    const parentLevel3 = activeLink.closest('.ez-toc-list-level-3');
                    if (parentLevel3) {
                        parentLevel3.classList.add('has-active-link');
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    };

    // Options for the IntersectionObserver
    const options = {
        root: null,
        threshold: 0.5,
    };

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
        // Add click event listener to TOC links
        document.querySelectorAll('.ez-toc-link').forEach(link => {
            link.addEventListener('click', function() {
                removeActiveClasses();
                this.classList.add('active');
                const parentLevel3 = this.closest('.ez-toc-list-level-3');
                if (parentLevel3) {
                    parentLevel3.classList.add('has-active-link');
                }
            });
        });

        // Create the observer for TOC links
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver(callback, options);
        document.querySelectorAll('.ez-toc-link').forEach(link => {
            // Updated to handle IDs starting with a digit
            const hrefAttribute = link.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
            const target = document.querySelector(`[id="${hrefAttribute}"]`);
            if (target) {
                observer.observe(target);
            }
        });
    });

window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    var stickyNav = document.querySelector('.sticky-nav-scrolling-up');
    var regularNav = document.querySelector('.navigation-stick');
    var tableOfContent = document.querySelector('.table-of-content-col');

    if (stickyNav && tableOfContent) {
        var stickyNavTop = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(stickyNav).getPropertyValue('top'), 10);
       	
        if (stickyNavTop > -145) {
            var newTopValue = 197 + stickyNavTop;
            tableOfContent.style.top = newTopValue + 'px';
       
        } 
    }
    else {	
        var stickyNavTop = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(regularNav).getPropertyValue('top'), 10);
        var newTopValue = 197 + stickyNavTop;
        tableOfContent.style.top = newTopValue + 'px';
    }
});

</script>
